  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=5.8)
    The story demonstrates technical control over poetic language and conceptual cohesion, but sacrifices human-scale emotional resonance for allegorical weight. The tight word count prevents full realization of character psychology despite thematic ambition. Lingering questions about existential self-perception hint at depth but feel designed more for cleverness than genuine contemplation.

  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=6.0)
